---
about_this_resource_text: "<p>In this lecture, Prof. Szolovits talks about algorithmic\
  \ fairness and fairness in the way we build machine learning models. He raises the\
  \ question &quot;What do we mean by fairness in society?&quot; and discusses how\
  \ that affects prediction models.</p>\r\n<p>Speaker: Peter Szolovits</p>\r\n   \
  \         <p><a href=\"./resolveuid/da43f26664d8e6bf6b0ae754bd656e6a\">Lecture 23:\
  \ Fairness slides (PDF - 1.5MB)</a></p>\r\n"
course_id: 6-s897-machine-learning-for-healthcare-spring-2019

  <span m="2034060">persisting.</span> <span m="2034750">There's</span> <span m="2035020">plenty</span>

  <span m="2042380">for</span> <span m="2042550">example,</span> <span m="2043400">take</span>

  <span m="2322805">A</span> <span m="2323090">versus</span> <span m="2323570">class</span>
  <span m="2323930">B.</span> <span m="2327430">That's</span> <span m="2327670">a</span>
  <span m="2327730">pretty</span> <span m="2328030">strong</span> <span m="2328510">requirement.</span></p><p><span
  m="2329920">And</span> <span m="2330100">then</span> <span m="2331150">you</span>
  <span m="2331330">can</span> <span m="2332500">operationalize</span> <span m="2333670">the</span>
  <span m="2333790">notion</span> <span m="2334240">of</span> <span m="2334390">unfairness</span>
  <span m="2335770">either</span> <span m="2336130">by</span> <span m="2336370">looking</span>
  <span m="2336760">for</span> <span m="2337030">an</span> <span m="2337120">absolute</span>
  <span m="2337690">difference</span> <span m="2338740">between</span> <span m="2339250">those</span>
  <span m="2339580">probabilities.</span> <span m="2340930">If</span> <span m="2341110">it's</span>
  <span m="2341290">greater</span> <span m="2341680">than</span> <span m="2341890">some</span>
  <span m="2342160">epsilon,</span> <span m="2343310">then</span> <span m="2343450">you</span>
  <span m="2343570">have</span> <span m="2343810">evidence</span> <span m="2344320">that</span>
  <span m="2344530">this</span> <span m="2344740">is</span> <span m="2344890">not</span>
  <span m="2345160">a</span> <span m="2345220">fair</span> <span m="2345490">scoring</span>
  <span m="2345970">function,</span> <span m="2347380">or</span> <span m="2347890">a</span>
  <span m="2347950">ratio</span> <span m="2348490">test</span> <span m="2349090">that</span>
  <span m="2349360">says,</span> <span m="2351100">we</span> <span m="2351280">look</span>
  <span m="2351520">at</span> <span m="2351640">the</span> <span m="2351760">ratio,</span>
  <span m="2352580">and</span> <span m="2352630">if</span> <span m="2352840">it</span>
  <span m="2352900">differs</span> <span m="2353470">from</span> <span m="2353800">1</span>
  <span m="2354610">significantly,</span> <span m="2356020">then</span> <span m="2356260">you</span>
  <span m="2356410">have</span> <span m="2356590">evidence</span> <span m="2357160">that</span>
  <span m="2357400">this</span> <span m="2357640">is</span> <span m="2357790">an</span>
  <span m="2358180">unfair</span> <span m="2358570">scoring</span> <span m="2359020">function.</span>
  <span m="2360140">And</span> <span m="2360190">by</span> <span m="2360340">the</span>
  <span m="2360430">way,</span> <span m="2360680">this</span> <span m="2360820">relates</span>
  <span m="2361330">to</span> <span m="2361480">the</span> <span m="2361600">4/5</span>
  <span m="2362320">rule,</span> <span m="2363130">because</span> <span m="2363550">if</span>
  <span m="2363700">you</span> <span m="2363820">make</span> <span m="2364120">epsilon</span>
  <span m="2366040">20%,</span> <span m="2368590">then</span> <span m="2368830">that's</span>
  <span m="2369130">the</span> <span m="2369220">same</span> <span m="2369550">as</span>
  <span m="2369730">the</span> <span m="2369820">4/5</span> <span m="2370360">rule.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2488410">can't</span> <span m="2488710">be</span> <span m="2488890">separated.</span>

  <span m="2491560">independent</span> <span m="2492280">of</span> <span m="2492400">each</span>
  <span m="2492580">other.</span> <span m="2494820">Now,</span> <span m="2495140">how</span>
  <span m="2495320">do</span> <span m="2495410">you</span> <span m="2495590">achieve</span>
  <span m="2496070">independence?</span> <span m="2497540">Well,</span> <span m="2497780">there</span>
  <span m="2497930">are</span> <span m="2497960">a</span> <span m="2497990">number</span>
  <span m="2498350">of</span> <span m="2498440">different</span> <span m="2498800">techniques.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2501170">is--</span> <span m="2502400">there's</span> <span m="2502850">this</span>
  <span m="2504260">article</span> <span m="2504740">by</span> <span m="2504950">Zemel</span>
  <span m="2506030">about</span> <span m="2506330">learning</span> <span m="2506690">fair</span>
  <span m="2506960">representations,</span> <span m="2508670">and</span> <span m="2508820">what</span>
  <span m="2509000">it</span> <span m="2509120">says</span> <span m="2510080">is</span>
  <span m="2510770">you</span> <span m="2511220">create</span> <span m="2512300">a</span>
  <span m="2512390">new</span> <span m="2512750">world</span> <span m="2512840">representation,</span>
  <span m="2514640">Z,</span> <span m="2515810">which</span> <span m="2516110">is</span>
  <span m="2516230">some</span> <span m="2516680">combination</span> <span m="2517580">of</span>
  <span m="2517700">X</span> <span m="2518000">and</span> <span m="2518150">A,</span>
  <span m="2519845">and</span> <span m="2520300">you</span> <span m="2520450">do</span>
  <span m="2520720">this</span> <span m="2521560">by</span> <span m="2521800">maximizing</span>
  <span m="2522850">the</span> <span m="2522970">mutual</span> <span m="2523480">information</span>
  <span m="2524290">between</span> <span m="2524770">X</span> <span m="2525130">and</span>
  <span m="2525280">Z</span> <span m="2526480">and</span> <span m="2526660">by</span>
  <span m="2526870">minimizing</span> <span m="2527800">the</span> <span m="2527890">mutual</span>
  <span m="2528370">information</span> <span m="2529270">between</span> <span m="2529760">the</span>
  <span m="2529810">A</span> <span m="2530125">and</span> <span m="2530440">Z.</span>
  <span m="2532410">So</span> <span m="2532590">this</span> <span m="2532830">is</span>
  <span m="2533010">an</span> <span m="2533130">idea</span> <span m="2533610">that</span>
  <span m="2533790">I've</span> <span m="2534000">seen</span> <span m="2534360">used</span>
  <span m="2534930">in</span> <span m="2535770">machine</span> <span m="2536190">learning</span>

  <span m="2540150">than</span> <span m="2540390">for</span> <span m="2540570">fairness,</span>
  <span m="2541740">where</span> <span m="2541980">people</span> <span m="2542340">say,</span>
  <span m="2543450">the</span> <span m="2543570">problem</span> <span m="2543990">is</span>
  <span m="2544230">that</span> <span m="2544530">given</span> <span m="2544920">a</span>
  <span m="2544980">particular</span> <span m="2545550">data</span> <span m="2545750">set,</span>
  <span m="2546210">you</span> <span m="2546330">can</span> <span m="2546510">overfit</span>
  <span m="2547080">to</span> <span m="2547230">that</span> <span m="2547470">data</span>
  <span m="2547680">set,</span> <span m="2548940">and</span> <span m="2549090">so</span>
  <span m="2549330">one</span> <span m="2549540">of</span> <span m="2549660">the</span>
  <span m="2549810">ideas</span> <span m="2550470">is</span> <span m="2550650">to</span>
  <span m="2550770">do</span> <span m="2551040">a</span> <span m="2551520">Gann-like</span>
  <span m="2552900">method</span> <span m="2553470">where</span> <span m="2553740">you</span>
  <span m="2553890">say,</span> <span m="2554700">I</span> <span m="2554820">want</span>
  <span m="2555030">to</span> <span m="2555090">train</span> <span m="2555480">my</span>
  <span m="2556020">classifier,</span> <span m="2556800">let's</span> <span m="2557040">say,</span>
  <span m="2557790">not</span> <span m="2558090">only</span> <span m="2558360">to</span>
  <span m="2558570">work</span> <span m="2558900">well</span> <span m="2559860">on</span>
  <span m="2560340">getting</span> <span m="2560730">the</span> <span m="2560820">right</span>
  <span m="2561090">answer,</span> <span m="2562050">but</span> <span m="2562260">also</span>
  <span m="2562650">to</span> <span m="2562830">work</span> <span m="2563190">as</span>
  <span m="2563370">poorly</span> <span m="2563790">as</span> <span m="2563970">possible</span>
  <span m="2565110">on</span> <span m="2565500">identifying</span> <span m="2567210">which</span>
  <span m="2567680">data</span> <span m="2567970">set</span> <span m="2568830">my</span>
  <span m="2569100">example</span> <span m="2569610">came</span> <span m="2569910">from.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2571730">the</span> <span m="2571820">same</span> <span m="2572120">sort</span>
  <span m="2572390">of</span> <span m="2572510">idea.</span> <span m="2572960">It's</span>
  <span m="2573140">a</span> <span m="2573170">representation</span> <span m="2574070">learning</span>
  <span m="2574460">idea.</span> <span m="2575480">And</span> <span m="2575660">then</span>
  <span m="2575900">you</span> <span m="2576080">build</span> <span m="2576890">your</span>
  <span m="2577100">predictor,</span> <span m="2577940">R,</span> <span m="2578780">based</span>
  <span m="2579260">on</span> <span m="2579560">this</span> <span m="2579830">representation,</span>
  <span m="2581360">which</span> <span m="2581690">is</span> <span m="2582050">perhaps</span>
  <span m="2582620">not</span> <span m="2582890">perfectly</span> <span m="2583730">independent</span>
  <span m="2585110">of</span> <span m="2585410">the</span> <span m="2585620">protected</span>
  <span m="2586220">attribute,</span> <span m="2586940">but</span> <span m="2587240">is</span>
  <span m="2587540">as</span> <span m="2587780">independent</span> <span m="2588470">as</span>
  <span m="2588620">possible.</span> <span m="2589920">And</span> <span m="2589970">usually,</span>
  <span m="2590510">there</span> <span m="2590690">are</span> <span m="2590780">knobs</span>
  <span m="2591290">in</span> <span m="2591410">these</span> <span m="2591650">learning</span>
  <span m="2592040">algorithms,</span> <span m="2592790">and</span> <span m="2592940">depending</span>
  <span m="2593450">on</span> <span m="2593630">how</span> <span m="2593810">you</span>
  <span m="2593960">turn</span> <span m="2594260">the</span> <span m="2594380">knob,</span>
  <span m="2595190">you</span> <span m="2595370">can</span> <span m="2595550">affect</span>
  <span m="2597500">whether</span> <span m="2597890">you're</span> <span m="2598070">going</span>
  <span m="2598260">to</span> <span m="2598340">get</span> <span m="2598550">a</span>
  <span m="2598610">better</span> <span m="2598940">classifier</span> <span m="2599810">that's</span>
  <span m="2600110">more</span> <span m="2600350">discriminatory</span> <span m="2601790">or</span>
  <span m="2601910">a</span> <span m="2602030">worse</span> <span m="2602330">classifier</span>
  <span m="2603140">that's</span> <span m="2603410">less</span> <span m="2603650">discriminatory.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="2606420">do</span> <span m="2606600">that</span> <span m="2607440">in</span>
  <span m="2607650">pre-processing.</span> <span m="2609720">You</span> <span m="2609930">can</span>
  <span m="2610170">do</span> <span m="2611490">some</span> <span m="2611760">kind</span>

  <span m="2880740">you</span> <span m="2880890">would</span> <span m="2881070">like.</span>
  <span m="2881980">So</span> <span m="2882120">for</span> <span m="2882300">example,</span>
  <span m="2882880">if</span> <span m="2882930">it's</span> <span m="2883140">a</span>
  <span m="2883170">coin</span> <span m="2883500">flip,</span> <span m="2884430">then</span>
  <span m="2884670">you'd</span> <span m="2884850">have</span> <span m="2885060">the</span>
  <span m="2885180">diagonal</span> <span m="2885810">line</span> <span m="2886770">and</span>
  <span m="2886920">the</span> <span m="2887070">only</span> <span m="2887310">feasible</span>
  <span m="2887880">region</span> <span m="2888330">would</span> <span m="2888540">be</span>
  <span m="2888720">below</span> <span m="2889080">that</span> <span m="2889290">diagonal,</span>
  <span m="2890760">no</span> <span m="2890970">matter</span> <span m="2891270">how</span>
  <span m="2891510">good</span> <span m="2891750">the</span> <span m="2891900">predictor</span>
  <span m="2892440">was</span> <span m="2892770">for</span> <span m="2892950">the</span>
  <span m="2893100">other</span> <span m="2893310">class.</span> <span m="2894490">So</span>
  <span m="2894570">that's</span> <span m="2894840">a</span> <span m="2894900">nice</span>
  <span m="2895230">characteristic.</span></p><p><span m="2897770">And</span> <span
  m="2897920">then</span> <span m="2898070">the</span> <span m="2898160">final</span>
  <span m="2898730">criterion</span> <span m="2899630">is</span> <span m="2899840">sufficiency,</span>
  <span m="2901440">which</span> <span m="2901850">flips</span> <span m="2902390">R</span>
  <span m="2902630">and</span> <span m="2902720">Y.</span> <span m="2903140">So</span>
  <span m="2903410">it</span> <span m="2903530">says</span> <span m="2903860">that</span>
  <span m="2904580">the</span> <span m="2905450">regressor</span> <span m="2906000">or</span>
  <span m="2906140">the</span> <span m="2906320">predictive</span> <span m="2906800">variable</span>
  <span m="2907400">can</span> <span m="2907670">depend</span> <span m="2908150">on</span>
  <span m="2908270">the</span> <span m="2908360">protected</span> <span m="2908960">class,</span>
  <span m="2910730">but</span> <span m="2911030">the</span> <span m="2911150">protected</span>
  <span m="2911750">class</span> <span m="2912140">is</span> <span m="2912230">separated</span>
  <span m="2912890">from</span> <span m="2913130">the</span> <span m="2913250">outcome.</span>
  <span m="2914910">So</span> <span m="2915080">for</span> <span m="2915260">example,</span>
  <span m="2916590">the</span> <span m="2916670">probability</span> <span m="2918680">in</span>
  <span m="2919100">a</span> <span m="2919160">binary</span> <span m="2919670">case</span>
  <span m="2920150">of</span> <span m="2920330">a</span> <span m="2920390">true</span>
  <span m="2920750">outcome</span> <span m="2921200">of</span> <span m="2921440">Y</span>
  <span m="2923750">given</span> <span m="2924260">that</span> <span m="2924740">R</span>
  <span m="2925070">is</span> <span m="2925340">some</span> <span m="2925610">particular</span>
  <span m="2926240">value,</span> <span m="2926790">R</span> <span m="2927170">and</span>
  <span m="2927470">A</span> <span m="2927740">is</span> <span m="2928820">a</span>
  <span m="2928910">particular</span> <span m="2929480">class,</span> <span m="2930470">is</span>
  <span m="2930680">the</span> <span m="2930800">same</span> <span m="2931310">as</span>
  <span m="2931520">the</span> <span m="2931640">probability</span> <span m="2932810">of</span>
  <span m="2932960">that</span> <span m="2933170">same</span> <span m="2933500">outcome</span>
  <span m="2933980">given</span> <span m="2934340">the</span> <span m="2934460">same</span>
  <span m="2934910">R</span> <span m="2936530">value,</span> <span m="2937550">but</span>
  <span m="2937745">the</span> <span m="2937940">different</span> <span m="2938330">class.</span>
  <span m="2940740">So</span> <span m="2940950">that's</span> <span m="2941250">related</span>
  <span m="2941910">to</span> <span m="2943350">the</span> <span m="2943950">sort</span>
  <span m="2944340">of</span> <span m="2944430">similar</span> <span m="2944940">people,</span>
  <span m="2945420">similar</span> <span m="2945900">treatment</span> <span m="2947730">notion,</span>
  <span m="2949830">qualitative</span> <span m="2950490">notion,</span> <span m="2950910">again.</span></p><p><span
  m="2953790">So</span> <span m="2954030">it</span> <span m="2954120">requires</span>
  <span m="2955405">a</span> <span m="2955670">parody</span> <span m="2956490">of</span>
  <span m="2956700">both</span> <span m="2957030">the</span> <span m="2957120">positive</span>
  <span m="2957750">and</span> <span m="2957870">the</span> <span m="2957990">negative</span>
  <span m="2958470">predictive</span> <span m="2958980">values</span> <span m="2959760">across</span>
  <span m="2960180">different</span> <span m="2960540">groups.</span> <span m="2963230">So</span>
  <span m="2963440">that's</span> <span m="2964940">another</span> <span m="2965360">popular</span>
  <span m="2965870">way</span> <span m="2966290">of</span> <span m="2966440">looking</span>
  <span m="2966830">at</span> <span m="2966950">this.</span> <span m="2968310">So</span>
  <span m="2968780">for</span> <span m="2968990">example,</span> <span m="2969540">if</span>
  <span m="2969570">the</span> <span m="2969680">scoring</span> <span m="2970100">function</span>

  <span m="3162410">So</span> <span m="3162550">this</span> <span m="3162790">was</span>
